Jinu's Demo Version!\nHopefully with this we can now get some concrete ideas on what this project will look like.\nThis is based off Exploration #1, and it is short but do try everything.\n\nAlso check out both left and right rooms from the corridor cuz i just randomly put some Twine functionality stuff in there.\nAlso make sure to go to the end of the corridor.\n\n[[This is completely for you.|Arrival]]\n\n<<silently>>\n$sanity = 1000\n\n<<endsilently>>\n
<<silently>>\n$sanity = 1000\n<<endsilently>>\n\n\tYour task is to explore a house. It’s a far cry from your usual repertoire of mountains and other extreme locales, but this one is a personal request from Reston. You’d think it was an elaborate prank if not for the tape that he sent you. “The Five and a Half Minute Hallway”, huh? It sounds like complete nonsense. Either way, if he’s telling the truth than he found the perfect man for the job. A discovery like this would make you a celebrity.\n\nStep into the [[house|Arrival1-2]].
\tAt long last, you and your crew free yourselves from the pestering of the house’s occupants and prepare to enter the hallway. You stow your rifle for now, instead arming yourself with a video camera and a powerful flashlight. Jed is in charge of maintaining radio contact with Navidson and company. The plan is to go to the end of the hallway, or at least as far in as two miles of fishing line will allow for. \n\tEnter the [[hallway|Hallway]].\n
\tYou brought two employees along, Jed and Wax, to help with this job. They keep laughing as the homeowner, Navidson, warns them of the dangers of the hallway and passes out copies of his crudely drawn map. Your focus is mostly on his beautiful wife, Karen. Besides, what does a photographer know about exploration anyway? Pulitzer prizes aren’t going to make anything easier. [[Let the professionals handle this|Arrival1-3]].\n\n
You arrive at Ash Tree Lane with a truck full of exploration supplies - mostly standard stuff, outside of a great spool of fishing line and a bundle of magnesium flares. You even brought your rifle, a beautiful Weatherby 300. Not that you’ll need it for [[this expedition|Arrival1-1]], of course.
<<silently>>\n$curLocation = 0\n$hallwayCount = 0\n<<display "macroDisplay">>\n<<origDisp>>\n<<endsilently>>\n[>img[short_1]]\nAll your doubts are set aside when you open the latches to the hallway and step inside. What strikes you most is the temperature. It’s cold, far more than you would expect.\n\n[[Step further inside|loopHall+]]
